<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 40.85pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=54>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>1<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 184.3pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=246>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>郑州博雅讯科技有限公司<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 3cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=113>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>马春龙<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>1</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、长期拖欠工资不发，最长拖过三个月，社保是满一年才给交。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR>2</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、罚钱很随便，从来不按照员工手册来，都是老板张口就来。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>3</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、喜欢下班开会，迟到也会扣钱。会强制安排员工干不是其岗位的工作，不干罚钱</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>4</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、喜欢节假日<SPAN class=GramE>喊员工</SPAN>干活，曾经清明节未放假，过年放假期间让员工来开会，五一放假期间让来搬家，而且这些都会算成你正常应该上的班，不会给你额外的工资和加班费，你不服从会给你按旷工。每逢放假前后就会让你连上十几天的班，把放的假都补回来。平时加班也是默认没有加班费。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>5</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、老板平时就是喜欢盯着员工，找员工的事，想办法罚你点钱，比如盯着带没带工牌，没带罚款。员工手册更是奇葩的很，几乎都是罚款的项目，比如迟到</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>10</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>分钟罚款</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>10</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>元，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>20</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>分钟罚款</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>20</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，半小时直接扣你半天工资。日志第一次没写扣款</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>10</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>块，第二次扣款</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>20</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，第三次</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>30</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，以此类推。每个月请假不能超过四天，超过会扣除一半绩效。就连你不改登录密码都会罚你钱，请年假都会扣除你全勤。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>6</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、老板喜欢开除价值不大的员工，但是不会说直接开除你，会给你降薪，调岗，威胁你等<SPAN class=GramE>等</SPAN>手段逼你自动离职。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>7</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、员工流动性极大，招不到人，一个岗位招几个月招<SPAN class=GramE>不</SPAN>来人，招来了干几天就跑，老板非常无耻，招聘时会骗你公司的有各种福利待遇，把你骗进来干活。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 155.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=208>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>有员工已经劳动仲裁该公司了</SPAN></P></TD></TR>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 40.85pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=54>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 184.3pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=246>

<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>黄黎明<SPAN lang=EN-US>(</SPAN>老板<SPAN lang=EN-US>)<BR></SPAN>陈鹏<SPAN lang=EN-US>(</SPAN>总经理<SPAN lang=EN-US>)<o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>高管都是骗子，鼓励员工在公司刷夜，经常洗脑，工资拖欠</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>(</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>曾上过新闻</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>,&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>但结果并未解决</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>)</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，程序员能给你逼成销售，无论试用期还是转正都签一份合同，还是公司留存。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>去面试过安卓，让三个小时内做一个支付宝的理财页面，开发软件自己下载，网速很慢，一个小时软件还没下载完，就走了，公司看着人挺多，感觉和外包一样，拼命肝的感觉</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 155.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=208>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 40.85pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=54>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 184.3pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=246>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN class=GramE><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>纬创盈通</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 3cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=113></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>1</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、技术部被一个不懂技术的二把刀子产品管着，不懂技术还喜欢指挥你，最爱说的话是这个问题一行代码就解决了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>!</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>喜欢打小报告，在电脑上安装监控软件，时刻窥探你。任何需求都一口应承，然后甩给技术，做不出来就是你不行，喜欢刺激的请积极踊跃投递简历</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR>2</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、产品当技术部领导，可想公司有多业余，而且这个产品也是二把刀子半路出家，三十多了，人品不敢恭维，怕自己被辞退，疯狂打压技术，把技术说的一无是处，开发换了一茬又一茬只有他不动，因为公司除了他谁都不能完全了解项目（项目已经上线运营），等不到开发了解项目，他就把人挤兑走，这样他的地位越来越稳固</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR>3</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、尤其擅长打小报告，下班你不加班他说你思想不积极，你加班出去吃饭时间长说你故意拖延，总之，爱吹枕边风</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR>4</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、办公电脑</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>U</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>盘不能用，不能连外网，需要用外网要申请，电脑装的都有监控软件，可以截屏、录屏、监控文件拷贝。公司</SPAN><SPAN class=SpellE><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>wifi</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>监控访问的网址，曾有人上班<SPAN class=GramE>用微信被</SPAN>罚款、辞退。啧啧<SPAN class=GramE>啧</SPAN>，酸爽</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>5</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、老子去面试过，面试完我就觉得有点坑，他们说做智慧城市的，我说想看看做到什么样了，他们支支吾吾半天也没说让看，吹的特别大</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 155.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=208>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>这是同一个公司！这是同一个公司！这是同一个公司！小刀是姓马的老板，<SPAN class=GramE>纬创是他</SPAN>亲戚的公司，他招聘以两个公司名义招，两个公司在一个屋办公。对求职者来说，<SPAN class=GramE>发同一个</SPAN>招聘当然是同一个公司，而且发的</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>offer</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>、工资也是以<SPAN class=GramE>纬创盈通</SPAN>的名义发的，只是老板和他亲戚自己算账，所以这两个招聘都是同一个项目组</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>老板姓马，产品姓李，<SPAN class=GramE>纬创集团</SPAN>是正规的，<SPAN class=GramE>纬创盈通</SPAN>是下边的子公司，<SPAN class=GramE>纬创盈通</SPAN>里又包括了一个本身的项目组和小刀项目组，小刀项目<SPAN class=GramE>组老板</SPAN>姓马，发的招聘是以小刀的名义发，也以微<SPAN class=GramE>创盈通</SPAN>的名义发。<SPAN class=GramE>纬创盈通</SPAN>里边那个吴姓的发的还可以，那个项目组是正常的，小刀这个不可以，为了掩饰，他会以<SPAN class=GramE>纬创盈通名义发</SPAN>招聘，注意甄别</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
<TR style="mso-yfti-irow: 12">
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 40.85pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=54>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>12<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 184.3pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=246>

<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>常年一直招人，外包，加班多，外派为主，面试基本上也很难过。工资是底薪加提成，底薪就两三千，没项目就没提成，而且做</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>863</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>公司自己的项目时候没有提成。还有大部分是外派到其他城市做项目，公司普通员工辞职率很高，大概半年就能换一遍</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>(se2</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>级别以上，在不在项目都是有工资，工资发送准时</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>..<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>我擦，我当时去面试了，好像在</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>16</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>层，说的特别大，还是什么国企，五险<SPAN class=GramE>一</SPAN>金，结果面了也没结果，今天看来幸好当时没去</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>是一个贷催收公司，入职<SPAN class=GramE>后东西</SPAN>做完立马解散，说公司没钱了，<SPAN class=GramE>做项目</SPAN>时<SPAN class=GramE>还要签投名状</SPAN>，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>40%</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，无偿加班不是正规软件公司，没有五险，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>签合同只有一份，公司保留着员工没有，随意开除人，几个人的公司还勾心斗角，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>开个会差一点<SPAN class=GramE>撸</SPAN>袖子打起来，姓赵的老总心知肚明就是不劝架，夏天开个空调他看到会</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; <TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>拖欠工资，公司有钱也盈利了就是不发。经常性拖三个月，到最后给结清了。但是拖欠，公司制度不行。在公司，<SPAN class=GramE>同事之间</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>沟通的话题永远都是：什么时候发工资，听说</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>XX</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>地方的项目回款了，公司主要是做政府各设区市平台建设的。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>

<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>赵梦<SPAN lang=EN-US>/</SPAN>杨志越<SPAN lang=EN-US>/</SPAN><SPAN class=GramE>王利强</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 155.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=208>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 3cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=113></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>垃圾外包公司，常年招聘对日外包，去了得学习日语一个月，学习期间没有工资，学习完了不干还得给他们几千块培训费。。。。。。这家公司还搞培训，忽悠培训！！</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>公司工资死低，离职各种理由拖欠工资不发，外包一线城市工资</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>5000</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，二线城市</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>4000</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，还不管吃住，没有五险<SPAN class=GramE>一</SPAN>金，没外包出去的没有工资拿，没有比<SPAN class=GramE>他更坑的</SPAN>，万恶的人力外包。面试水的要命，面试官不懂技术，拿着一个小本本念面试<SPAN class=GramE>题问</SPAN>，狗子都能进去。。。。。。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>

<P style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 12pt; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>要了简历，学<SPAN class=GramE>信网截</SPAN>图，然后给发了一个有云计划</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>标签的简历，之后就没下文了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>兄弟</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>,</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>你这是坑了吧</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>...</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>表面是软件公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>,</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>其实是培训机构，<SPAN class=GramE>云计划</SPAN>还有个霸王条款，合同内只能公司辞你，而你不能辞职，自己辞职需要赔偿公司两万元，，，这条违反国家法律，不用理会，拿着这玩意直接起诉就行。就是起诉周期可能有点长</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR>

COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>我就没答应去，然后公司人事各种劝说，非让我再去一趟</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>在商量商量，拗不过，就又去了一趟结果还是那样，过了几天</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>估计没找到合适的人，又苦口婆心的说啊</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>什么兼职也行，<SPAN class=GramE>让我估一下</SPAN>多少钱，看人家<SPAN class=GramE>挺</SPAN>诚心的，我就估了一下，跟他说了之后，以后就再不劝我了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>估计被吓着了还是怎么着，其实<SPAN class=GramE>一</SPAN>项目我才说了一万五而已，人事前后态度反差之大，很是不解。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>这个公司在<SPAN class=GramE>郑州九博和</SPAN>智联上可能会搜到，当初没投他们公司简历，自己查到的就给我打电话让来面试，面试说最近有个<SPAN class=GramE>活比较</SPAN>急，着急招人来写，当时找了好久都没找到工作，就答应了，刚来的时候还挺好的，后来人多了，活也不好做，估计感觉养不起了，就开始拖工资，本来是</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>15</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>号发，有的时候拖个</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>3,4</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>天也没啥，后来越来越久，直接拖了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>2</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>个月，有个人就受不了问，然后老板每次都说过几天就发，员工们都没心情写代码了，想着<SPAN class=GramE>不</SPAN>发工资就不写，老板就怒了，说谁不干活就</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>**</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，有人不服，吵了一架就走了，然而还是没法工资，老板还会在公司群里装</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>*</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>，结果是没发工资，还降了，唉</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>……<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 40.85pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=54>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>93<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 184.3pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=246>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>上海惠为信息技术有限公司，郑州分公司<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 3cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=113>
<P class=MsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" align=center><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>蒋东卿<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>说是什么分公司，其实啥也不是。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>有项目就招人，没项目就裁人。公司没有行政，没有任何福利待遇。每天无偿加班，甚至到十二点，周末说是双休基本上很少双休过。办公地点极其小，还是租甲方的一间小屋子，这么抠的公司见过么？这也算是上海的一个分公司？？？说是什么分公司老板，其实就是一个沙雕无脑自大的<SPAN class=GramE>傻逼男</SPAN>，叫蒋东卿。由于公司租的小房间太小，坐<SPAN class=GramE>不</SPAN>下人，就让我们回家办公，每天基本上</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>24</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>小时待命，每天不分时间点，随时给你发微信，<SPAN class=GramE>不秒回</SPAN>就打电话轰炸，甲方不看项目，他也不测试项目，甲方只要提出哪天看项目，他就测到后半夜，半夜给你打电话。每天发日报，不能直接发钉钉里，要先把<SPAN class=GramE>日报发群里</SPAN>，对着你的每条日报，逐字逐句的验证，验证通过才可以发往钉钉。每天随时随地，他都可能给你发微信，打电话，就跟他不让别人有个人生活，他也没有个人生活一样。经常把你干的活说的很简单，就说不就啥啥啥么，基本上每一天都恶心你，每天都让你弄的很糟心，你有啥好心情，都得被他弄的很糟。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>每个节日公司没有任何礼品，公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>不会有任何小聚，因为公司连群都没有。而且发工资没有工资条的，请假一天比正常工作日扣的钱都多的，只要你问他任何工作之外，福利待遇薪资相关的事，立马给你脸色看，给你阴阳怪气的。工作中就跟不信任你一样，你干的活每天必须经过给他验证成功，才可以发日报。就<SPAN class=GramE>一</SPAN>男人中的极品，<SPAN class=GramE>咋配结婚</SPAN>了，怕是小时候有童年阴影么</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>?</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>婚姻不幸福，对员工撒气么？但是人家对上海那边的人，跟他爹一样好</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><BR></SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>最后建议大家，千万不要来这家公司，就是个坑！！！</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 155.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=208>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 184.3pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=246>

<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 3cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=113></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 11cm; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=416>
<P class=MsoNormal style="mso-element: frame; mso-element-frame-hspace: 9.0pt; mso-element-wrap: around; mso-element-anchor-vertical: paragraph; mso-element-anchor-horizontal: column; mso-element-top: .05pt; mso-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>招聘的时候对外说是郑煤机的，说和郑煤机集团一样走国企待遇，现在是<SPAN class=GramE>赶项目</SPAN>加班，实际上根本不是，干了一段时间才签署合同，写的不定时工作制，每天</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>7</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>点</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>40</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>上班，上到下午</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>17</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>点半，当初说忙完就是双休和国企待遇一致走节假日正常，实际上根本不是，<SPAN class=GramE>固定单</SPAN>休，节假日缩水，清明</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>3</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>天休</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>2</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>天，五一</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'>5</SPAN><SPAN style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #24292f; mso-ascii-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: "Segoe UI"; mso-bidi-font-family: "Segoe UI"'>天休三天，本来的周日单休休息还被叫过来培训，各种人上人的打压你，你下班走了还要被大喇叭等领导背后说闲话，说不加班等，还有人奉承国企关系的领导，加班在办公室熬点，每次领导走了再走</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style='FONT-FAMILY: "Segoe UI",sans-serif; COLOR: #24292f'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
<TD style="BORDER-TOP: medium none; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 155.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: medium none; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" width=208>
